\n    46→    field2 == VALUE2;\n    47→  });\n    48→  \n    49→  // 4. Set configuration handle\n    50→  req.apb_master_agent_cfg_h = p_sequencer.apb_master_a

apb_master_seq_pkg\n    71→```\n    72→\n    73→## APB Transaction Fields\n    74→\n    75→The `apb_master_tx` transaction has these key fields:\n    76→\n    7
7→- **`pwrite`**: Operation type - `WRITE` or `READ`\n    78→- **`transfer_size`**: Data width - `BIT_8`, `BIT_16`, `BIT_24`, or `BIT_32`\n    79→- **`pselx`**:
 Slave selection - `SLAVE_0`, `SLAVE_1`, etc.\n    80→- **`paddr`**: Address (randomized by default)\n    81→- **`pwdata`**: Write data (randomized by default)\
n    82→\n    83→## Common Constraint Patterns\n    84→\n    85→### Fixed transfer size and operation:\n    86→```systemverilog\n    87→assert(req.randomize() w
ith {\n    88→  transfer_size == BIT_8;\n    89→  pwrite == WRITE;\n    90→});\n    91→```\n    92→\n    93→### Specific slave:\n    94→```systemverilog\n    95
→assert(req.randomize() with {\n    96→  pselx == SLAVE_0;\n    97→});\n    98→```\n    99→\n   100→## UVM Factory Pattern\n   101→\n   102→Always use `type_id:
:create()` to instantiate objects:\n   103→```systemverilog\n   104→req = apb_master_tx::type_id::create(\"req\");\n   105→```\n   106→\n   107→This enables UVM
 factory overrides for better reusability.\n   108→\n   109→## Configuration Objects\n   110→\n   111→Sequences receive configuration from the sequencer via `p_
sequencer.apb_master_agent_cfg_h`. Always pass this to your transactions:\n   112→```systemverilog\n   113→req.apb_master_agent_cfg_h = p_sequencer.apb_master_a
gent_cfg_h;\n   114→```\n   115→\n   116→## Running Simulations\n   117→\n   118→From `repo/sim/cadence_sim/`:\n   119→```bash\n   120→make simulate TEST=apb_8b
